\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00533}00533\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Speed\ are\ per-\/pixel\ of\ mouse\ movement\ (v\_speed=0.2f:\ mouse\ needs\ to\ move\ by\ 5\ pixels\ to\ increase\ value\ by\ 1).\ For\ gamepad/keyboard\ navigation,\ minimum\ speed\ is\ Max(v\_speed,\ minimum\_step\_at\_given\_precision).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00534}00534\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Use\ v\_min\ <\ v\_max\ to\ clamp\ edits\ to\ given\ limits.\ Note\ that\ CTRL+Click\ manual\ input\ can\ override\ those\ limits\ if\ ImGuiSliderFlags\_AlwaysClamp\ is\ not\ used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l00535}00535\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Use\ v\_max\ =\ FLT\_MAX\ /\ INT\_MAX\ etc\ to\ avoid\ clamping\ to\ a\ maximum,\ same\ with\ v\_min\ =\ -\/FLT\_MAX\ /\ INT\_MIN\ to\ avoid\ clamping\ to\ a\ minimum.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01142}01142\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ When\ using\ auto-\/resizing\ (non-\/resizable)\ fixed\ columns,\ querying\ the\ content\ width\ to\ use\ item\ right-\/alignment\ e.g.\ SetNextItemWidth(-\/FLT\_MIN)\ doesn't\ make\ sense,\ would\ create\ a\ feedback\ loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01143}01143\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ -\/\ Using\ Stretch\ columns\ OFTEN\ DOES\ NOT\ MAKE\ SENSE\ if\ ScrollX\ is\ on,\ UNLESS\ you\ have\ specified\ a\ value\ for\ 'inner\_width'\ in\ BeginTable().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01144}01144\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ If\ you\ specify\ a\ value\ for\ 'inner\_width'\ then\ effectively\ the\ scrolling\ space\ is\ known\ and\ Stretch\ or\ mixed\ Fixed/Stretch\ columns\ become\ meaningful\ again.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01145}01145\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Read\ on\ documentation\ at\ the\ top\ of\ imgui\_tables.cpp\ for\ details.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01172}\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba6f36a3c3aff05b68a46d42f53e287c2c}{01172}}\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba6f36a3c3aff05b68a46d42f53e287c2c}{ImGuiTableFlags\_SizingStretchProp}}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 3\ <<\ 13,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Columns\ default\ to\ \_WidthStretch\ with\ default\ weights\ proportional\ to\ each\ columns\ contents\ widths.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01174}01174\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Sizing\ Extra\ Options}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01175}\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba7150c6964021a048b8379aed41e0205a}{01175}}\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba7150c6964021a048b8379aed41e0205a}{ImGuiTableFlags\_NoHostExtendX}}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 16,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Make\ outer\ width\ auto-\/fit\ to\ columns,\ overriding\ outer\_size.x\ value.\ Only\ available\ when\ ScrollX/ScrollY\ are\ disabled\ and\ Stretch\ columns\ are\ not\ used.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01176}\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dbae0d8a05a918fdb4e917d2e0e9ee4b008}{01176}}\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dbae0d8a05a918fdb4e917d2e0e9ee4b008}{ImGuiTableFlags\_NoHostExtendY}}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 17,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Make\ outer\ height\ stop\ exactly\ at\ outer\_size.y\ (prevent\ auto-\/extending\ table\ past\ the\ limit).\ Only\ available\ when\ ScrollX/ScrollY\ are\ disabled.\ Data\ below\ the\ limit\ will\ be\ clipped\ and\ not\ visible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01177}\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba9676cbb7244d6e74e7d312d28326af7b}{01177}}\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba9676cbb7244d6e74e7d312d28326af7b}{ImGuiTableFlags\_NoKeepColumnsVisible}}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 18,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Disable\ keeping\ column\ always\ minimally\ visible\ when\ ScrollX\ is\ off\ and\ table\ gets\ too\ small.\ Not\ recommended\ if\ columns\ are\ resizable.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01178}\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dbac0541efd539e873cb39dd3f82bb7e210}{01178}}\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dbac0541efd539e873cb39dd3f82bb7e210}{ImGuiTableFlags\_PreciseWidths}}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 19,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Disable\ distributing\ remainder\ width\ to\ stretched\ columns\ (width\ allocation\ on\ a\ 100-\/wide\ table\ with\ 3\ columns:\ Without\ this\ flag:\ 33,33,34.\ With\ this\ flag:\ 33,33,33).\ With\ larger\ number\ of\ columns,\ resizing\ will\ appear\ to\ be\ less\ smooth.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01179}01179\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Clipping}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01180}\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba212d615067ef6f3bac0b8acf64b5358f}{01180}}\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba212d615067ef6f3bac0b8acf64b5358f}{ImGuiTableFlags\_NoClip}}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 20,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Disable\ clipping\ rectangle\ for\ every\ individual\ columns\ (reduce\ draw\ command\ count,\ items\ will\ be\ able\ to\ overflow\ into\ other\ columns).\ Generally\ incompatible\ with\ TableSetupScrollFreeze().}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01181}01181\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Padding}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01183}\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dbad7f3d4694dbfdcb47e21dad9da0cb742}{01183}}\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dbad7f3d4694dbfdcb47e21dad9da0cb742}{ImGuiTableFlags\_NoPadOuterX}}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 22,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Default\ if\ BordersOuterV\ is\ off.\ Disable\ outermost\ padding.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01184}\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba4603f87c3e531d83a40fba8764077fbf}{01184}}\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba4603f87c3e531d83a40fba8764077fbf}{ImGuiTableFlags\_NoPadInnerX}}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 23,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Disable\ inner\ padding\ between\ columns\ (double\ inner\ padding\ if\ BordersOuterV\ is\ on,\ single\ inner\ padding\ if\ BordersOuterV\ is\ off).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01185}01185\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Scrolling}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{imgui_8h_source_l01186}\mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba9844889ae8d1b7d9737b7488436dc8ec}{01186}}\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{imgui_8h_ade214f01f7eda181bb321fb5d59457dba9844889ae8d1b7d9737b7488436dc8ec}{ImGuiTableFlags\_ScrollX}}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 24,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Enable\ horizontal\ scrolling.\ Require\ 'outer\_size'\ parameter\ of\ BeginTable()\ to\ specify\ the\ container\ size.\ Changes\ default\ sizing\ policy.\ Because\ this\ creates\ a\ child\ window,\ ScrollY\ is\ currently\ generally\ recommended\ when\ using\ ScrollX.}}
